The survivors wander, drawn to a blooming light in the distance.
They find the serene comfort of a towering pile of lanterns and a
result on the back of the settlement record sheet. Choose and

time during the settlement phase.

to Returning Survivors.
The First Day settlement event card will not be used again during
this campaign. Do not include it in your settlement event deck.
